<h1 _ngcontent-nna-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.fastbuffer (FastBuffer)"> @ohos.fastbuffer (FastBuffer) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>FastBuffer对象是更高效的Buffer容器，用于表示固定长度的字节序列，是专门存放二进制数据的缓存区。</p>    <p>FastBuffer通过from构造时，仅支持FastBuffer、Uint8Array、string、Array、ArrayBuffer类型的参数。</p>    <p>需要高性能处理大型二进制数据（如图片、文件传输、网络通信等）时，推荐使用FastBuffer。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 20开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>      <p>容器类使用静态语言实现，限制了存储位置和属性，不支持自定义属性和方法。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 999px;">     <h2 id="bufferencoding" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">BufferEncoding<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bufferencoding" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type BufferEncoding = 'ascii' | 'utf8' | 'utf-8' | 'utf16le' | 'ucs2' | 'ucs-2' | 'base64' | 'base64url' | 'latin1' | 'binary' | 'hex'</p>     <p>表示支持的编码格式类型。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.6.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ascii'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示ascii格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf8'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf8格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf-8'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf8格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'utf16le'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示utf16小端序格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ucs2'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">utf16le格式的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'ucs-2'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">utf16le格式的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'base64'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示base64格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'base64url'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示base64url格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'latin1'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">iso-8859-1的别名，向下兼容ascii格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'binary'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示二进制格式。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">'hex'</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示十六进制格式。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1235px;">     <h2 id="fastbufferalloc" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.alloc<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbufferalloc" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>alloc(size: number, fill?: string | FastBuffer | number, encoding?: BufferEncoding): FastBuffer</p>     <p>创建指定字节长度的FastBuffer对象并初始化。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的FastBuffer对象长度，单位：字节。取值范围：0 &lt;= size &lt;= UINT32_MAX。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">fill</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | FastBuffer | number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">填充至新缓存区的值，默认值：0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">编码格式（当fill为string时，才有意义）。默认值：'utf8'。传入无法识别的encoding会抛出TypeError。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个FastBuffer对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbufferallocuninitializedfrompool" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>allocUninitializedFromPool(size: number): FastBuffer</p>     <p>从缓冲池中创建指定大小未初始化的FastBuffer对象，需要使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fill">fill</a>函数来初始化FastBuffer对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version  <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的FastBuffer对象长度，单位：字节。取值范围：0 &lt;= size &lt;= UINT32_MAX。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">未初始化的Buffer实例。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 953px;">     <h2 id="fastbufferallocuninitialized" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.allocUninitialized<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbufferallocuninitialized" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>allocUninitialized(size: number): FastBuffer</p>     <p>创建指定大小未初始化的FastBuffer对象，需要使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fill">fill</a>函数来初始化FastBuffer对象。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">size</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定的FastBuffer对象长度，单位：字节。取值范围：0 &lt;= size &lt;= UINT32_MAX。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1190px;">     <h2 id="fastbufferbytelength" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.byteLength<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbufferbytelength" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>byteLength(value: string | FastBuffer | TypedArray | DataView | ArrayBuffer | SharedArrayBuffer, encoding?: BufferEncoding): number</p>     <p>根据不同的编码格式，返回指定字符串的字节数。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | FastBuffer | TypedArray | DataView | ArrayBuffer | SharedArrayBuffer</td>         <td class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1289px;">     <h2 id="fastbuffercompare" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.compare<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbuffercompare" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>compare(buf1: FastBuffer | Uint8Array, buf2: FastBuffer | Uint8Array): -1 | 0 | 1</p>     <p>返回两个FastBuffer对象的比较结果，通常用于对FastBuffer对象数组进行排序。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">buf1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a> | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">待比较的第一个对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">buf2</td>         <td      <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">待比较的第二个对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-1 | 0 | 1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>如果buf1与buf2相同，则返回0。</p>          <p>如果排序时buf1位于buf2之后，则返回1。</p>          <p>如果排序时buf1位于buf2之前，则返回-1。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> <h2 id="fastbufferconcat" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.concat<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>concat(list: FastBuffer[] | Uint8Array[], totalLength?: number): FastBuffer</p>     <p>将数组中指定字节长度的内容复制到新的FastBuffer对象中并返回拼接后的FastBuffer对象。</p>     <p>当数组中所有对象的长度总和大于totalLength时，返回结果的长度将被截断为totalLength。</p>     <p>当数组中所有对象的长度总和小于totalLength时，返回结果的多余部分将会被填充为0。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字节长度， 默认值:（arrayBuffer.byteLength - byteOffset）。取值范围：0 &lt;= length &lt;= arrayBuffer.byteLength - byteOffset</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.14.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个FastBuffer对象，该对象与入参对象arrayBuffer共享相同的内存区域。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a <h2 id="fastbufferfrom-2" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.from<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>from(buffer: FastBuffer | Uint8Array): FastBuffer</p>     <p>当入参为FastBuffer对象时，创建新的FastBuffer对象并复制入参FastBuffer对象的数据，然后返回新对象。</p>     <p>当入参为Uint8Array对象时，基于Uint8Array对象的内存创建新的FastBuffer对象并返回，保持数据的内存关联。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">buffer</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a> | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">对象数据。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fastbuffer.transcode<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fastbuffertranscode" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>transcode(source: FastBuffer | Uint8Array, fromEnc: string, toEnc: string): FastBuffer</p>     <p>将FastBuffer或Uint8Array对象从fromEnc编码转换为toEnc编码。</p>     <p>fastbuffer.transcode支持的编码：'ascii' | 'utf8' | 'utf16le'| 'ucs2' | 'latin1'| 'binary'。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">source</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a> | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">实例对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">fromEnc</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">当前编码。 支持的格式范围为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">toEnc</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">目标编码。 支持的格式范围为<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"  </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1927px;">     <h3 id="compare" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">compare<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="compare" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>compare(target: FastBuffer | Uint8Array, targetStart?: number, targetEnd?: number, sourceStart?: number, sourceEnd?: number): -1 | 0 | 1</p>     <p>比较当前对象this与目标对象target，并返回比较结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr> Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要比较的实例对象。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">target实例中开始的偏移量。默认值：0。 0 &lt;= targetStart &lt;= target.length。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">targetEnd</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">target实例中结束的偏移量（不包含结束位置）。默认值：目标对象的字节长度。取值范围：0 &lt;= targetEnd &lt;= target.length。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sourceStart</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">this实例中结束的偏移量（不包含结束位置）。默认值：当前对象的字节长度。取值范围：0 &lt;= sourceEnd &lt;= this.length。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.22.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">-1 | 0 | 1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>返回比较结果。</p>          <p>-1：当前排列在目标前；</p>          <p>0：当前与目标相同；</p>          <p>1：当前排列在目标后。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div> <p>将this实例中指定位置的数据复制到target的指定位置上，并返回复制的字节总长度。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p> id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>   <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于填充的值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">offset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">起始偏移量。默认值：0。取值范围：0 &lt;= offset &lt;= this.length。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">end</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">结束偏移量（不包含结束位置）。 默认值：当前对象的字节长度。取值范围：0 &lt;= end &lt;= this.length。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字符编码格式（value为string才有意义）。默认值：'utf8'。传入无法识别的encoding会抛出TypeError。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#fastbuffer">FastBuffer</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回填充后的FastBuffer对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-utils">语言基础类库错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> Possible causes: The value of the parameter is not within the specified range.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">10200068</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">The underlying ArrayBuffer is null or detach.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { fastbuffer } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkTS'</span>;</li><li>

style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1323px;">     <h3 id="includes" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">includes<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="includes" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>includes(value: string | number | FastBuffer | Uint8Array, byteOffset?: number, encoding?: BufferEncoding): boolean</p>     <p>检查FastBuffer对象是否包含value值。</p>     <p>若byteOffset为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；如果为负数，则从末尾开始计算偏移量。</p>     <p>当byteOffset大于等于this.length时，返回false。当byteOffset小于等于-this.length，查找整个FastBuffer中是否存在value。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | number | FastBuffer | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要搜索的内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">byteOffset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字节偏移量。若为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；若byteOffset为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；如果为负数，则从末尾开始计算偏移量。默认值：0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字符编码格式。默认值：'utf8'。传入无法识别的encoding会抛出TypeError。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">若FastBuffer对象包含value值时返回true，否则为false。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">indexOf<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="indexof" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>indexOf(value: string | number | FastBuffer | Uint8Array, byteOffset?: number, encoding?: BufferEncoding): number</p>     <p>返回当前对象中首次出现value的索引，如果不包含value，则返回-1。</p>     <p>若byteOffset为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；如果为负数，则从末尾开始计算偏移量。</p>     <p>当byteOffset大于等于this.length时，返回-1。当byteOffset小于等于-this.length，返回整个FastBuffer中首次出现value的索引。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>   <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要查找的内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">byteOffset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>   </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1299px;">     <h3 id="lastindexof" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">lastIndexOf<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="lastindexof" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>lastIndexOf(value: string | number | FastBuffer | Uint8Array, byteOffset?: number, encoding?: BufferEncoding): number</p>     <p>返回当前对象中最后一次出现value的索引，如果对象不包含value，则返回-1。</p>     <p>若byteOffset为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；如果为负数，则从末尾开始计算偏移量。</p>     <p>当byteOffset大于等于this.length时，返回整个FastBuffer中最后一次出现value的索引。当byteOffset小于等于-this.length时，返回-1。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | number | FastBuffer | Uint8Array</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要搜索的内容。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">byteOffset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字节偏移量。若byteOffset为正数，则从0开始计算偏移量；如果为负数，则从末尾开始计算偏移量。默认值：this.length - 1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-fastbuffer#bufferencoding">BufferEncoding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字符编码格式。默认值：'utf8'。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.31.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">最后一次出现value值的索引。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.54.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">start</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">截取开始位置。默认值：0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">end</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">截取结束位置（不包含结束位置）。默认值：当前对象的字节长度。取值范围：start &lt;= end &lt;= this.length</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr <p>将当前对象中指定位置的数据转成指定编码格式的字符串并返回。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">encoding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">字符编码格式。默认值：'utf8'。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">start</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">结束位置。默认值：Buffer.length。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.59.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">字符串。当start &gt;= this.length或start &gt; end时返回空字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> underlying ArrayBuffer is null or detach.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div width="25%">偏移量。默认值：0。取值范围：0 &lt;= offset &lt;= this.length - byteLength。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">byteLength</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要写入的字节数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.81.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">偏移量offset加上写入的字节数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-utils">语言基础类库错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> out of range. Received value is: [param]</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-nna-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { fastbuffer } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkTS'</span>;</li><li>

result);</li><li><span class="hljs-comment">// 输出结果：result = 6</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1326px;">     <h3 id="writeuintle" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">writeUIntLE<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="writeuintle" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>writeUIntLE(value: number, offset: number, byteLength: number): number</p>     <p>在FastBuffer对象的offset偏移处写入小端序的无符号数据，字节长度为byteLength。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.82.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.82.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.82.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.82.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">写入Buffer的数据。取值范围取决于byteLength。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">offset</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">偏移量。默认值：0。取值范围：0 &lt;= offset &lt;= this.length - byteLength。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">byteLength</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">要写入的字节数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>
